<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлев.html>хлев</a> (17868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xlěvъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлев.html>хлев</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlev</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлев.html>хле́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлев.html>хлева́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлев.html>хлево́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stable, stall, cowshed</li>
<li>sheep cote</li>
<li>pigsty, pigpen</li></ol>

***хлестать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хлеста́ть</a> (7040)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлыст.html>хлыст</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlyst</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хлеста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlestátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестнуть.html>хлестну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хлестану́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lash, to switch, to whip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хлеста́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веник.html>ве́ником</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баня.html>ба́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xlestátʹ</b> vénikom v báne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat with birch twigs in the bathhouse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to beat down <i>(on)</i>, to lash <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хле́щет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ <b>xléščet</b> v oknó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rain is beating down (on) the window panes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хле́щет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ <b>xléščet</b> nam v licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rain is beating in our faces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кровь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хле́щет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рана.html>ра́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krovʹ <b>xléščet</b> iz rány</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blood is gushing from the wound</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хле́щет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ tak i <b>xléščet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rain is lashing down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guzzle <i>(down)</i>, to glug</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлестнуть.html>хлестну́ть</a> (14713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хлеста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlestátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестнуть.html>хлестну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlestnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хлеста́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lash, to switch, to whip</li></ol>

***хлипкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлипкий.html>хли́пкий</a> (22029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Dialectally also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хли́бкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlíbkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хлибко́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlibkój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хли́бый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlíbyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xlibъkъ</i>. Cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хли́бать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlíbatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall ill, to shake from weakness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хли́бить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlíbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлипкий.html>хли́пкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlípkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хли́пче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> weak, fragile, flimsy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frail, sickly, puny</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shaky, unsteady</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> weak-willed, spineless</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> watery, diluted</li></ol>

***хлоп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлоп.html>хлоп</a> (18737)</h1><br><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крестьянин.html>крестья́нин</a> n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Между тем в русском стане началась безурядица и смятение. … Между <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">хлопами</span> на сходках стали ходить такие речи: татары разоряют край наш; выдадим королю старшину и будем свободны. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Она понимала, о каком «расчете» говорил Корчагин. Ей была известна вся история с петлюровцами, но желание подразнить этого <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">«хлопа»</span> толкало ее на издевку. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>
</body>

***хлопать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a> (3346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlópatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопнуть.html>хло́пнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похлопать.html>похло́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xlópatʹ</b> v ladóši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to clap one’s hands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to flap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́льями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xlópatʹ</b> krýlʹjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flap one's wings</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to slap, to smack; to crack (a whip)</li>
<li>to tap</li>
<li>to slam (a door)</li>
<li>to bang, to <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>pop</a></li></ol>

<li>(no equivalent)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлопец.html>хло́пец</a> (7374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хло́пець</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlópecʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boy, lad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">chłopiec</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопец.html>хло́пец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlópec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопец.html>хло́пца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопец.html>хло́пцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопец.html>хло́пцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lad, boy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навеки.html>наве́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:умолкнуть.html>умо́лкли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>весёлые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопец.html>хло́пцы</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живы́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a>.</i> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:орленок.html>Орлёнок</a>" - "Eaglet", <i>a song of the Soviet period</i>)<dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Navéki umólkli vesjólyje <b>xlópcy</b>, v živýx ja ostálsja odín.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The merry lads got silent for ever, I was the only one who survived.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холоп.html>холо́п</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xolóp</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>serf, slave, bondman; peasant</i>)</li></ul>

***хлопнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлопнуть.html>хло́пнуть</a> (2618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlópatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопнуть.html>хло́пнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlópnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flap, to clap</li>
<li>to slam (door)</li></ol>

<ol><li>n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Изобразить, сочинить обиду и уйти и, может быть, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">хлопнуть</span>, и это бы совсем хорошо, то есть <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">хлопнуть</span> дверью, а дальше уже по телефону и с расстояния; дальше уже проще. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>выпить (спиртной напиток) <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***хлопотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлопотать.html>хлопота́ть</a> (7192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">клопотъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klopotŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">клопота́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klopotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">клопотя́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klopotjá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring to tears</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">klороtаti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопотать.html>хлопота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlopotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похлопотать.html>похлопота́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захлопотать.html>захлопота́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bustle about, to diligently do things</li>
<li>to hustle, to fuss</li>
<li>to try to achieve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопотать.html>хлопочи́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>xlopočíte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't bother</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to try to help, to intercede (for), to plead (for) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually with the authorities</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлорка.html>хло́рка</a> (28409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хло́рный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хло́рная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlórnaja ízvestʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bleach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлорка.html>хло́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлорка.html>хло́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлорка.html>хло́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлорка.html>хло́рок</a></b>)

***хлынуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлынуть.html>хлы́нуть</a> (7578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлынуть.html>хлы́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlýnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to gush out, to spout</li>
<li>to pour, to flood
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1884</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sofia_Kovalevskaya" class="extiw" title="w:Sofia Kovalevskaya">Sofia Kovalevskaya</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9D%D0%B8%D0%B3%D0%B8%D0%BB%D0%B8%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BA%D0%B0" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Нигилистка">Nihilist</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">васи́льцев <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диван.html>дива́на</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штора.html>што́ру</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отворить.html>отвори́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>лучи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудный.html>чу́дного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весенний.html>весе́ннего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлынуть.html>хлы́нули</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сноп.html>снопо́м</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vasílʹcev vstal s divána, podnjál štóru i otvoríl oknó. Pérvyje lučí čudnovo vesénnevo utra <b>xlýnuli</b> snopóm.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Vasiltsev got up from the sofa, raised the blind and opened the window. The first rays of a wonderful spring morning <b>came flooding</b> in a shaft of light.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***хлыст.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлыст.html>хлыст</a> (17900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoetic according to Vasmer. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлестать.html>хлеста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlestátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">chłosta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлыст.html>хлыст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xlyst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлыст.html>хлыста́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлыст.html>хлысты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлыст.html>хлысто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>whip, switch (thin rod used as a whip)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Khlyst (a member of an underground sect from late 17th to early 20th century that split off from the Russian Orthodox Church)</li></ol>

***хлюпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлюпать.html>хлю́пать</a> (12115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хлюп</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xljup</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлюпать.html>хлю́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xljúpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squelch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flounder, to squelch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлюпать.html>хлю́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xljúpatʹ</b> po grjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">squelch through the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sniffle, to snuffle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хлюпать.html>хлю́пать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>но́сом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xljúpatʹ</b> nósom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sniff</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***хлястик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлястик.html>хля́стик</a> (28877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлястик.html>хля́стик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xljástik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлястик.html>хля́стика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлястик.html>хля́стики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлястик.html>хля́стиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strap; long narrow strip of cloth or leather used to hold something like a piece of clothing or headwear, or a part of some equipment or furniture</li></ol>

***хмелеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хмелеть.html>хмеле́ть</a> (32455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмель.html>хмель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xmelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хмелеть.html>хмеле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xmelétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">охмеле́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:захмелеть.html>захмеле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become intoxicated, to drunk, to tipsy or high</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become exhilarated</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xъmelь</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
